8
# Monster Name	id	image[,image...]	Monster Parameters	drop 1	drop2	...
#
# Prefixes for item drop rates:
# p - pickpocket only (assumed 5% rate).
# n - no pickpocket.
# c - conditional item drop (which implies no pickpocket) - basically a
# reminder that you may need to do something (like talk to Grandpa) to
# make this item eligible to drop.
# f - fixed rate drop, +item modifiers have no effect.
# m - multidrop, multiple items at the same time. We assume these are not
# pickpocketable because if you pickpocket them you get exactly 1 item and
# they don't drop after combat, but some are pickpocketable in-game.
# a - stealable accordion

# Regular monsters

# Dreadsylvania
#
# http://kolspading.com/forums/viewtopic.php?f=2&t=403
#
# Bugbear: HP: [600+KW*200] Atk: [400+KW*100] Def: [400+KW*100] Init: [15+KW*10]
# Werewolf: HP: [max(500,1.25*(MUS+(KW-2)*10))] Atk: [max(400,MOX+(KW-2)*10))] Def: [max(400,MUS+(KW-2)*10))] Exp: [(max(400,STAT+(KW-2)*10)))/4] Init: [15+KW*10]
# Zombie: HP: [600+KV*200] Atk: [400+KV*100] Def: [400+KV*100] Init: [15+KV*10]
# Ghost: HP: [600+KV*200] Atk: [400+KV*100] Def: [400+KV*100] Init: [15+KV*10]
# Vampire: HP: [600+KC*200] Atk: [400+KC*100] Def: [400+KC*100] Init: [15+KC*10]
# Skeleton: HP: [1000*2^(KC-1)] Atk: [400+KC*100] Def: [400+KC*100] Init: [15+KC*10]
#
# Hot: Init: [15+K*60]
# Cold: (K-1) turns of Chilled to the Bone
# Sleaze: chance to fumble
# Stench: environmental damage + (K-1) turns of Nauseated
# Spooky: (K-1) turns of curse
